Console input: {

Console input: {
Console input: if(string[i] < '0' || string[i] > '9')
Console input: {
Console input: return 0; // It's not a number, return 0 (false)
Console input: }
Console input: }
Console input: return 1; // It's a number, return 1 (true)
Console input: }

Console input: public GetVehicleName(vehicleid, model[], len)
Console input: {
Console input: new checking = GetVehicleModel(vehicleid);
Console input: if(checking == 400) return format(model, len, "Landstalker", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 401) return format(model, len, "Bravura", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 402) return format(model, len, "Buffalo", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 403) return format(model, len, "Linerunner", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 404) return format(model, len, "Perenail", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 405) return format(model, len, "Sentinel", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 406) return format(model, len, "Dumper", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 407) return format(model, len, "Firetruck", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 408) return format(model, len, "Trashmaster", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 409) return format(model, len, "Stretch", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 410) return format(model, len, "Manana", 0);
Console input: else if(checking == 411) return format(model, len, "Infernus", 0);

Console input: public OnCheckPlayerData(playerid)
Console input: {
Console input: // Check if result has atleast one row, that means player has an account, show him dialog for login
Console input: if(cache_num_rows() > 0)
Console input: {
Console input: cache_get_value_name(0, "Password", PlayerInfo[playerid][Password], 65);
Console input: cache_get_value_name(0, "Salt", PlayerInfo[playerid][Salt], 11);
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_LOGIN, DIALOG_STYLE_PASSWORD, "Login", "Vas nalog je pronadjen. Molimo Vas upisite lozinku da se prijavite", "Dalje", "Izlaz");
Console input: }
Console input: // Otherwise, player is not registered, show him dialog for registration
Console input: else
Console input: {
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_REGISTER, DIALOG_STYLE_PASSWORD, "Registracija", "Vas nalog nije pronadjen. Molimo Vas upisite lozinku da se registrujete", "Dalje", "Izlaz");
Console input: }
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }

Console input: public SendRadiusMessage(Float:radius, playerid, string[], color1, color2, color3, color4, color5)
Console input: {
Console input: new Float:X, Float:Y, Float:Z, Float:OX, Float:OY, Float:OZ, Float:MSGX, Float:MSGY, Float:MSGZ;
Console input: new PlayerVirtualWorld = GetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid);
Console input: GetPlayerPos(playerid, OX, OY, OZ);
Console input: for(new i = 0; i < MAX_PLAYERS; i++)
Console input: {
Console input: if(PlayerVirtualWorld != GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i)) return 1;
Console input: GetPlayerPos(i, X, Y, Z);
Console input: MSGX = (OX - X);
Console input: MSGY = (OY - Y);
Console input: MSGZ = (OZ - Z);
Console input: if(((MSGX < radius/16) && (MSGX > -radius/16)) && ((MSGY < radius/16) && (MSGY > -radius/16)) && ((MSGZ < radius/16) && (MSGZ > -radius/16))) SendClientMessage(i, color1, string);
Console input: else if(((MSGX < radius/8) && (MSGX > -radius/8)) && ((MSGY < radius/8) && (MSGY > -radius/8)) && ((MSGZ < radius/16) && (MSGZ > -radius/8))) SendClientMessage(i, color2, string);
Console input: else if(((MSGX < radius/4) && (MSGX > -radius/4)) && ((MSGY < radius/4) && (MSGY > -radius/4)) && ((MSGZ < radius/16) && (MSGZ > -radius/4))) SendClientMessage(i, color3, string);
Console input: else if(((MSGX < radius/2) && (MSGX > -radius/2)) && ((MSGY < radius/2) && (MSGY > -radius/2)) && ((MSGZ < radius/2) && (MSGZ > -radius/2))) SendClientMessage(i, color4, string);
Console input: else if(((MSGX < radius) && (MSGX > -radius)) && ((MSGY < radius) && (MSGY > -radius)) && ((MSGZ < radius) && (MSGZ > -radius))) SendClientMessage(i, color5, string);
Console input: }
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: public StartVehicleEngine(playerid, vehicleid)
Console input: {
Console input: new engine, lights, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective, playername[MAX_PLAYER_NAME], str[128];
Console input: GetVehicleParamsEx(vehicleid, engine, lights, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective);
Console input: SetVehicleParamsEx(vehicleid, 1, 1, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective);
Console input: VehicleEngine[vehicleid] = 1;
Console input: StartingVehicleEngine[playerid] = 0;
Console input: TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 1);
Console input: SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "Motor vozila pokrenut.");
Console input: GetPlayerName(playerid, playername, sizeof(playername));
Console input: format(str, sizeof(str), "%s pali motor vozila.", playername);
Console input: SendRadiusMessage(50.0, playerid, str, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
Console input: }
Console input: public CheckVehicleFuel()
Console input: {
Console input: new engine, lights, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective;
Console input:     for(new v = 0; v < MAX_VEHICLES; v++)
Console input:     {

Console input: {
Console input: #pragma unused help
Console input: for(new i = 0; i < MAX_VEHICLES; i++) 
Console input: {
Console input: if(!IsARentVehicle(i)) continue;
Console input: new bool:PlayerInVehicle = false;
Console input: for(new j = 0; j < MAX_PLAYERS; j++)
Console input: {
Console input: if(!IsPlayerConnected(j)) continue;
Console input: if(!IsPlayerInVehicle(j, i)) continue;
Console input: PlayerInVehicle = true;
Console input: }
Console input: if(!PlayerInVehicle) SetVehicleToRespawn(i);
Console input: }
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }

Console input: {

Console input: }

Console input: public CheckPlayerData(playerid)
Console input: {
Console input: new query[128], playername[MAX_PLAYER_NAME];
Console input: GetPlayerName(playerid, playername, sizeof(playername));
Console input: mysql_format(mysql, query, sizeof(query), "SELECT Password, Salt FROM Players WHERE NAME = '%e' LIMIT 1", playername);
Console input: mysql_tquery(mysql, query, "OnCheckPlayerData", "i", playerid);
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: public OnCheckPlayerData(playerid)
Console input: {
Console input: // Check if result has atleast one row, that means player has an account, show him dialog for login
Console input: if(cache_num_rows() > 0)
Console input: {
Console input: cache_get_value_name(0, "Password", PlayerInfo[playerid][Password], 65);
Console input: cache_get_value_name(0, "Salt", PlayerInfo[playerid][Salt], 11);
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_LOGIN, DIALOG_STYLE_PASSWORD, "Login", "Vas nalog je pronadjen. Molimo Vas upisite lozinku da se prijavite", "Dalje", "Izlaz");
Console input: }
Console input: // Otherwise, player is not registered, show him dialog for registration
Console input: else
Console input: {
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_REGISTER, DIALOG_STYLE_PASSWORD, "Registracija", "Vas nalog nije pronadjen. Molimo Vas upisite lozinku da se registrujete", "Dalje", "Izlaz");
Console input: }
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: public LoadPlayerData(playerid)
Console input: {
Console input: new query[128], playername[MAX_PLAYER_NAME];
Console input: GetPlayerName(playerid, playername, sizeof(playername));
Console input: mysql_format(mysql, query, sizeof(query), "SELECT * FROM Players WHERE NAME = '%e' LIMIT 1", playername);
Console input: mysql_tquery(mysql, query, "OnLoadPlayerData", "i", playerid);
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: public OnLoadPlayerData(playerid)
Console input: {
Console input: // Check if result has atleast one row, that means player has an account, show him dialog for login
Console input: if(cache_num_rows() > 0)
Console input: {
Console input: cache_get_value_name_int(0, "ID", PlayerInfo[playerid][ID]);
Console input: cache_get_value_name(0, "Password", PlayerInfo[playerid][Password], 65);
Console input: cache_get_value_name(0, "Salt", PlayerInfo[playerid][Salt], 11);
Console input: cache_get_value_name_int(0, "Sex", PlayerInfo[playerid][Sex]);
Console input: cache_get_value_name_int(0, "Age", PlayerInfo[playerid][Age]);
Console input: cache_get_value_name_int(0, "Country", PlayerInfo[playerid][Country]);
Console input: cache_get_value_name_int(0, "City", PlayerInfo[playerid][City]);
Console input: cache_get_value_name_float(0, "SpawnX", PlayerInfo[playerid][SpawnX]);
Console input: cache_get_value_name_float(0, "SpawnY", PlayerInfo[playerid][SpawnY]);
Console input: cache_get_value_name_float(0, "SpawnZ", PlayerInfo[playerid][SpawnZ]);
Console input: }
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }

Console input: }

Console input: public SendRadiusMessage(Float:radius, playerid, string[], color1, color2, color3, color4, color5)
Console input: {
Console input: new Float:X, Float:Y, Float:Z, Float:OX, Float:OY, Float:OZ, Float:MSGX, Float:MSGY, Float:MSGZ;
Console input: new PlayerVirtualWorld = GetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid);
Console input: GetPlayerPos(playerid, OX, OY, OZ);
Console input: for(new i = 0; i < MAX_PLAYERS; i++)
Console input: {
Console input: if(PlayerVirtualWorld != GetPlayerVirtualWorld(i)) return 1;
Console input: GetPlayerPos(i, X, Y, Z);
Console input: MSGX = (OX - X);
Console input: MSGY = (OY - Y);
Console input: MSGZ = (OZ - Z);
Console input: if(((MSGX < radius/16) && (MSGX > -radius/16)) && ((MSGY < radius/16) && (MSGY > -radius/16)) && ((MSGZ < radius/16) && (MSGZ > -radius/16))) SendClientMessage(i, color1, string);
Console input: else if(((MSGX < radius/8) && (MSGX > -radius/8)) && ((MSGY < radius/8) && (MSGY > -radius/8)) && ((MSGZ < radius/16) && (MSGZ > -radius/8))) SendClientMessage(i, color2, string);
Console input: else if(((MSGX < radius/4) && (MSGX > -radius/4)) && ((MSGY < radius/4) && (MSGY > -radius/4)) && ((MSGZ < radius/16) && (MSGZ > -radius/4))) SendClientMessage(i, color3, string);
Console input: else if(((MSGX < radius/2) && (MSGX > -radius/2)) && ((MSGY < radius/2) && (MSGY > -radius/2)) && ((MSGZ < radius/2) && (MSGZ > -radius/2))) SendClientMessage(i, color4, string);
Console input: else if(((MSGX < radius) && (MSGX > -radius)) && ((MSGY < radius) && (MSGY > -radius)) && ((MSGZ < radius) && (MSGZ > -radius))) SendClientMessage(i, color5, string);
Console input: }
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }

Console input: public CheckVehicleFuel()
Console input: {
Console input: new engine, lights, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective;
Console input:     for(new v = 0; v < MAX_VEHICLES; v++)
Console input:     {
Console input:    GetVehicleParamsEx(v, engine, lights, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective);
Console input:     if(IsABoat(v)) VehicleFuel[v] += 1;
Console input:     if(IsAPlane(v)) VehicleFuel[v] += 1;
Console input:     if(VehicleEngine[v] == 1 && VehicleFuel[v] > 0) VehicleFuel[v] -= 1;
Console input:     if(VehicleFuel[v] < 1)
Console input: {
Console input: SetVehicleParamsEx(v, 0, 0, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective);
Console input: VehicleEngine[v] = 0;
Console input: }
Console input: }
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }

Console input: switch(dialogid)
Console input: {
Console input: case DIALOG_LOGIN:
Console input: {
Console input: if(!response)
Console input: {
Console input: return Kick(playerid);
Console input: }
Console input: new buffer[65], playername[MAX_PLAYER_NAME];
Console input: SHA256_PassHash(inputtext, PlayerInfo[playerid][Salt], buffer, 65);
Console input: if(strcmp(buffer, PlayerInfo[playerid][Password]) == 0)
Console input: {
Console input: GetPlayerName(playerid, playername, sizeof(playername));
Console input: LoadPlayerData(playerid);
Console input: // If player didnt pick Sex, show him dialog
Console input: if(!PlayerInfo[playerid][Sex])
Console input: {
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_SEX, DIALOG_STYLE_LIST, "Registracija - Pol", "Musko\nZensko", "U redu", "Izadji");
Console input: }
Console input: // If player didnt pick Age, show him dialog
Console input: else if(!PlayerInfo[playerid][Age])
Console input: {
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_AGE, DIALOG_STYLE_INPUT, "Registracija - Godine", "Unesite koliko imate godina", "U redu", "Izadji");
Console input: }
Console input: // If player didnt pick Country, show him dialog
Console input: else if(!PlayerInfo[playerid][Country])
Console input: {
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_COUNTRY, DIALOG_STYLE_LIST, "Registracija - Drzava", "Srbija\nCrna Gora\nBosna i Hercegovina\nHrvatska\nMakedonija\nOstalo", "U redu", "Izadji");
Console input: }
Console input: // If player didnt picky City, show him dialog
Console input: else if(!PlayerInfo[playerid][City])
Console input: {
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_CITY, DIALOG_STYLE_LIST, "Registracija - Grad", "Los Santos\nLas Venturas\nSan Fierro", "U redu", "Izadji");
Console input: }
Console input: // Otherwise, player is fully registered, spawn him
Console input: else 
Console input: {
Console input: SetSpawnInfo(playerid, 0, 0, PlayerInfo[playerid][SpawnX], PlayerInfo[playerid][SpawnY], PlayerInfo[playerid][SpawnZ], 360.0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0);
Console input: SpawnPlayer(playerid);
Console input: }
Console input: }
Console input: else
Console input: {
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_LOGIN, DIALOG_STYLE_PASSWORD, "Login", "Lozinka koju ste uneli nije ispravna, pokusajte ponovo", "Dalje", "Izlaz");
Console input: }
Console input: }
Console input: case DIALOG_REGISTER:
Console input: {
Console input: if(!response) 
Console input: {
Console input: return Kick(playerid);
Console input: }
Console input: if(strlen(inputtext) < 6 || strlen(inputtext) > 20)
Console input: {
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_REGISTER, DIALOG_STYLE_INPUT, "Registracija", "Vas nalog nije pronadjen. \nMolimo Vas upisite lozinku da se registrujete", "Dalje", "Izlaz");
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: for (new i = 0; i < 10; i++) 
Console input: {
Console input: PlayerInfo[playerid][Salt][i] = random(100) + 50;
Console input: }
Console input: PlayerInfo[playerid][Salt][10] = 0;
Console input: SHA256_PassHash(inputtext, PlayerInfo[playerid][Salt], PlayerInfo[playerid][Password], 65);
Console input: new query[256], playername[MAX_PLAYER_NAME];
Console input: GetPlayerName(playerid, playername, sizeof(playername));
Console input: mysql_format(mysql, query, sizeof(query), "INSERT INTO Players SET \
Console input: Name = '%e', \
Console input: Password = '%e', \
[21:38:37] Setting server password to: "= '%e', \"
Console input: Salt = '%e'", playername, PlayerInfo[playerid][Password], PlayerInfo[playerid][Salt]);
Console input: mysql_tquery(mysql, query, "OnPlayerRegister", "i", playerid);
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_SEX, DIALOG_STYLE_LIST, "Registracija - Pol", "Musko\nZensko", "U redu", "Izadji");
Console input: }
Console input: case DIALOG_SEX:
Console input: {
Console input: new query[256];
Console input: if(!response) 
Console input: {
Console input: return Kick(playerid);
Console input: }
Console input: if(listitem == 0)
Console input: {
Console input: PlayerInfo[playerid][Sex] = 1;
Console input: mysql_format(mysql, query, sizeof(query), "UPDATE Players \
Console input: SET Sex = %d \
Console input: WHERE ID = %d", PlayerInfo[playerid][Sex], PlayerInfo[playerid][ID]);
Console input: mysql_tquery(mysql, query);
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_AGE, DIALOG_STYLE_INPUT, "Registracija - Godine", "Unesite koliko imate godina", "U redu", "Izadji");
Console input: }
Console input: else if(listitem == 1)
Console input: {
Console input: PlayerInfo[playerid][Sex] = 2;
Console input: mysql_format(mysql, query, sizeof(query), "UPDATE Players \
Console input: SET Sex = %d \
Console input: WHERE ID = %d", PlayerInfo[playerid][Sex], PlayerInfo[playerid][ID]);
Console input: mysql_tquery(mysql, query);

Console input: }
Console input: }
Console input: case DIALOG_AGE:

Console input: }

Console input: {

Console input: }

Console input: }
Console input: years = strval(inputtext);
Console input: if(years < 7 || years > 99)
Console input: {
Console input: return ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_AGE, DIALOG_STYLE_INPUT, "Registracija - Godine", "Molimo Vas budite iskreni sa godinama. \nUnesite koliko imate godina.", "U redu", "Izadji");
Console input: }
Console input: mysql_format(mysql, query, sizeof(query), "UPDATE Players \

Console input: WHERE ID = %d", years, PlayerInfo[playerid][ID]);
Console input: mysql_tquery(mysql, query);
Console input: ShowPlayerDialog(playerid, DIALOG_COUNTRY, DIALOG_STYLE_LIST, "Registracija - Drzava", "Srbija\nCrna Gora\nBosna i Hercegovina\nHrvatska\nMakedonija\nOstalo", "U redu", "Izadji");

Console input: // ====================================================================================================== Commands
Console input: YCMD:avehicle(playerid, params[], help)
Console input: {
Console input: #pragma unused help 
Console input: new VehicleID, vehicle, color1, color2, Float:X, Float:Y, Float:Z;
Console input: if(sscanf(params, "iii", vehicle, color1, color2))
Console input: {
Console input: return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "[KORISCENJE]: /avehicle [id_vozila] [boja1] [boja2]");
Console input: }
Console input: GetPlayerPos(playerid, X, Y, Z);
Console input: VehicleID = CreateVehicle(vehicle, X+1, Y+1, Z, 270.0, color1, color2, -1);
Console input: VehicleEngine[VehicleID] = 0;
Console input: VehicleFuel[VehicleID] = 30;
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: /* YCMD:(playerid, params[], help)
Console input: {
Console input: #pragma unused help
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }*/
Console input: // Command that respawns all rent vehicles
Console input: // TO:DO - Check if player is admin
Console input: YCMD:respawnujrentvozila(playerid, params[], help)
Console input: {
Console input: #pragma unused help
Console input: for(new i = 0; i < MAX_VEHICLES; i++) 
Console input: {
Console input: if(!IsARentVehicle(i)) continue;
Console input: new bool:PlayerInVehicle = false;
Console input: for(new j = 0; j < MAX_PLAYERS; j++)
Console input: {
Console input: if(!IsPlayerConnected(j)) continue;
Console input: if(!IsPlayerInVehicle(j, i)) continue;
Console input: PlayerInVehicle = true;
Console input: }
Console input: if(!PlayerInVehicle) SetVehicleToRespawn(i);
Console input: }
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: YCMD:iznajmivozilo(playerid, params[], help)
Console input: {
Console input: #pragma unused help
Console input: new VehicleID;
Console input: if(!IsPlayerInAnyVehicle(playerid)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "[GRESKA]: Niste u vozilu!");
Console input: VehicleID = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
Console input: if(!IsARentVehicle(VehicleID)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "[GRESKA]: Niste u vozilu za iznajmljivanje!");
Console input: //if(GetPlayerMoney(playerid) < 50) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1 ,"[GRESKA]: Nemate dovoljno novca da iznajmite vozilo!");
Console input: if(IsPlayerRentingVehicle[playerid]) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "[GRESKA]: Vec ste iznajmili neko vozilo!");
Console input: for(new i = 0; i < MAX_PLAYERS; i++) 
Console input: {
Console input: if(RentedVehicle[i] == VehicleID) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "[GRESKA]: Neko je vec iznajmio ovo vozilo!");
Console input: }
Console input: IsPlayerRentingVehicle[playerid] = 1;
Console input: RentedVehicle[playerid] = VehicleID;
Console input:    TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 1);
Console input: SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "Iznajmili ste vozilo. Da vratite vozilo kucajte: /vrativozilo");
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: YCMD:vrativozilo(playerid, params[], help)
Console input: {
Console input: #pragma unused help
Console input: new VehicleID = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
Console input: if(!IsPlayerRentingVehicle[playerid]) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "[GRESKA]: Nemate iznajmljeno vozilo.");
Console input: if(VehicleID == RentedVehicle[playerid]) TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 1);
Console input: SetVehicleToRespawn(RentedVehicle[playerid]);
Console input: IsPlayerRentingVehicle[playerid] = 0;
Console input: RentedVehicle[playerid] = 0;
Console input: SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "Vratili ste iznajmljeno vozilo.");
Console input: return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: YCMD:motor(playerid, params[], help)
Console input: {
Console input: #pragma unused help
Console input: new playername[MAX_PLAYER_NAME], VehicleID, engine, lights, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective, Float:VehicleHealth, str[128];
Console input: if(!IsPlayerInAnyVehicle(playerid)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Niste u vozilu!");
Console input: VehicleID = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
Console input: GetVehicleParamsEx(VehicleID, engine, lights, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective);
Console input: if(IsASalesVehicle(VehicleID)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete pokrenuti motor ovog vozila!");
Console input: if(IsARentVehicle(VehicleID) && (IsPlayerRentingVehicle[playerid] == 0 || RentedVehicle[playerid] != VehicleID)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete pokrenuti motor ovog vozila!");
Console input: if(VehicleFuel[VehicleID] == 0) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Rezervoar je prazan!");
Console input: if(RefuellingVehicle[playerid] == 1) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Sipanje goriva u toku!");
Console input: if(VehicleEngine[VehicleID] == 0)
Console input: {
Console input:     GetVehicleHealth(VehicleID, VehicleHealth);
Console input:     if(VehicleHealth <= 500.0) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete upaliti motor vozila. Motor je ostecen!");
Console input:     if(StartingVehicleEngine[playerid] == 1) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Vec pokusavate da pokrenete motor vozila!");
Console input:     StartingVehicleEngine[playerid] = 1;
Console input:     TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 0);
Console input: SetTimerEx("StartVehicleEngine", 3500, false, "ii", playerid, VehicleID);
Console input:     GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~w~Pokretanje motora vozila...", 3500, 3);
Console input:     GetPlayerName(playerid, playername, sizeof(playername));
Console input:     format(str, sizeof(str), "%s okrece kljuc i pokusava da upali motor vozila.", playername);
Console input:     SendRadiusMessage(50.0, playerid, str, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
Console input: }
Console input: else
Console input: {
Console input:     SetVehicleParamsEx(VehicleID, 0, 0, alarm, doors, bonnet, boot, objective);
Console input:     VehicleEngine[VehicleID] = 0;
Console input:     SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "Ugasili ste motor vozila.");
Console input:     GetPlayerName(playerid, playername, sizeof(playername));
Console input:     format(str, sizeof(str), "%s gasi motor vozila.", playername);
Console input:     SendRadiusMessage(50.0, playerid, str, -1, -1, -1, -1, -1);
Console input:  }
Console input:     return 1;
Console input: }
Console input: YCMD:sipajgorivo(playerid, params[], help)
Console input: {
Console input: #pragma unused help
Console input: new VehicleID, litre, pump1, pump2, pump3;
Console input: if(sscanf(params, "i", litre)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "KORISCENJE: /sipajgorivo [litara] (x5$)");
Console input: if(!IsPlayerInAnyVehicle(playerid)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Niste u vozilu!");
Console input: VehicleID = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
Console input: pump1 = IsPlayerNearPump1(playerid);
Console input: pump2 = IsPlayerNearPump2(playerid);
Console input: pump3 = IsPlayerNearPump3(playerid);
Console input: if(pump1 != -1 && pump1 != 0)
Console input: {
Console input: if(VehicleEngine[VehicleID] == 1) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "Morate prvo ugasiti motor! (/engine)");
Console input: //if(GetPlayerMoney(playerid) < litre*5) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Nemate dovoljno novca da sipate gorivo! (litar 5$)");
Console input: if(IsABike(VehicleID) && litre + VehicleFuel[VehicleID] > 30) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete da sipate toliko goriva! (30l rezervoar)");
Console input: else if(litre + VehicleFuel[VehicleID] > 60) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete da sipate toliko goriva! (60l rezervoar)");
Console input: TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 0);
Console input: GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~w~PUNJENJE GORIVA...", 10000, 3);
Console input: SetTimerEx("AntiFreezePlayer", litre, false, "i", playerid);
Console input: RefuellingVehicle[playerid] = 1;
Console input: RefillLitre[playerid] = litre;
Console input: }
Console input: else if(pump2 != -1 && pump2 != 0)
Console input: {
Console input: if(VehicleEngine[VehicleID] == 1) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "Morate prvo ugasiti motor! (/engine)");
Console input: //if(GetPlayerMoney(playerid) < litre*5) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Nemate dovoljno novca da sipate gorivo! (litar 5$)");
Console input: if(IsABike(VehicleID) && litre + VehicleFuel[VehicleID] > 30) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete da sipate toliko goriva! (30l rezervoar)");
Console input: else if(litre + VehicleFuel[VehicleID] > 60) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete da sipate toliko goriva! (60l rezervoar)");
Console input: TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 0);
Console input: GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~w~PUNJENJE GORIVA...", 10000, 3);
Console input: SetTimerEx("AntiFreezePlayer", litre, false, "i", playerid);
Console input: RefuellingVehicle[playerid] = 1;
Console input: RefillLitre[playerid] = litre;
Console input: }
Console input: else if(pump3 != -1 && pump3 != 0)
Console input: {
Console input: if(VehicleEngine[VehicleID] == 1) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "Morate prvo ugasiti motor! (/engine)");
Console input: //if(GetPlayerMoney(playerid) < litre*5) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Nemate dovoljno novca da sipate gorivo! (litar 5$)");
Console input: if(IsABike(VehicleID) && litre + VehicleFuel[VehicleID] > 30) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete da sipate toliko goriva! (30l rezervoar)");
Console input: else if(litre + VehicleFuel[VehicleID] > 60) return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Ne mozete da sipate toliko goriva! (60l rezervoar)");
Console input: TogglePlayerControllable(playerid, 0);
Console input: GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~w~PUNJENJE GORIVA...", 10000, 3);
Console input: SetTimerEx("AntiFreezePlayer", litre, false, "i", playerid);
Console input: RefuellingVehicle[playerid] = 1;
Console input: RefillLitre[playerid] = litre;
Console input: }
Console input: else return SendClientMessage(playerid, -1, "GRESKA: Niste na pump!");

Console input: }
